Mysterious Lights of Diwali


30 Oct 2024

Mysterious Lights of Diwali




Light up with Mysterious Lighting Chair~

Mechanics


Top-up @Cash via FIUU, convert to Maple Cash and spend 100k @Cash between 30th October 2024, 0000hrs to 12th November 2024, 2359hrs (GMT +8) to walkaway with Mysterious Lighting Chair!


Click here to learn how to top-up @Cash with FIUU!
Happy Diwali~



Terms & Conditions


  • This promotion is open to FIUU customers only.
  • eWallet/QR Payment and Credit/Debit Card options are eligible to participate, as long as it's within the FIUU payment platform.
  • Customers must top-up the 100,000 @Cash denomination options in a single transaction with FIUU, convert @Cash to Maple Cash and subsequently spend Maple Cash in-game within the event period of 30th October 2024, 0000hrs to 12th November 2024, 2359hrs (GMT +8 to qualify for the Merchandise.
  • Spending must be done in a single MapleID within the MapleStorySEA Passport account that was used to charge with FIUU and converted to Maple Cash respectively.
  • Each MapleStorySEA Passport account will only receive a maximum of ONE (1) reward item.
  • In-game purchases that use a mix of Maple Cash and Mileage will be eligible, but only the Maple Cash portion will be counted.
  • All charging, conversion and spending of Maple Cash completed outside of the event period will NOT be entitled to receive the promotional items.
  • PlayPark Pte Ltd and Nexon Korea Corporation shall not be held responsible for any disputes over the event results or claim of prizes.
  • PlayPark Pte Ltd and Nexon Korea Corporation reserve the right to suspend or take action against any user found to breach the policies outlined in our Terms of Use, User Abuse Policy, and Rules of Conduct without any prior notice.
  • PlayPark Pte Ltd and Nexon Korea Corporation reserve the right to amend and/or remove the promotion and associating terms and conditions at its discretion without any prior notice.
  • All decisions by PlayPark Pte Ltd and Nexon Korea Corporation are final & binding.

    - MapleSEA Administrator

    • [Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 30th October 2024


    29 Oct 2024

    [Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 30th October 2024


    [Update as of 30th October 2024, 1324hrs (GMT +8)]

    The Server Check and Cash Shop Update has concluded and game services for all worlds have resumed at 1324hrs (GMT +8).

    Regarding Lost of Achievement's Progress Due to Urgent Maintenance on 14th October 2024

    Due to the service interruption, some Maplers are unable to complete check-in based achievement(s) on time which caused the achievement's progress being reset. We would like to apologize for not addressing this issue in our initial compensation plan on 16th October 2024.

    To address this issue, a data comparison between 14th October 2024 and 30th October 2024, before maintenance will be performed on the following achievements.
    â€ƒâ†ª Moras Honorary Citizen
    â€ƒâ†ª [Monster Park] Familiarity While Fighting
    â€ƒâ†ª Did you see that? Attendance Check done 15 times in a row!
    â€ƒâ†ª Did you see that? Attendance Check completed for 1 year
    If the achievement progress on 14th October 2024 is greater than 30th October 2024, before maintenance, the achievement progress will combine both data from 14th October 2024 and 30th October 2024, before maintenance.

    For example, the progress of Moras Honorary Citizen was 80 days on 14th October 2024 and 10 days on 30th October 2024, before maintenance. Since the data on 14th October 2024 is greater than 30th October 2024, before maintenance, both data will be combined and the current achievement progress becomes 90 days.

    Important Notice:
  • The combined achievement progress will not exceed the achievement's maximum progress value.
  • Maplers are advised to login to the affected character(s) after the maintenance has concluded to ensure the achievement's progress has been restored.

    • Error Fixes
  • An issue where Amazing Pink Bean/Yeti Complete Box cannot be claimed has been fixed. Maplers may claim the reward until 5th November 2024, 2359hrs.

    • Known Issue
  • An issue where Hayato's Hyoru Getsuken buff's stack(s) resets after the character resurrect is being investigated.
  • An issue when equipping/unequipping Breath of Divinity, multiple skills activation/deactivation appear as text notice is being investigated.
  • An issue where Equality Cube can be used on OTP Locked equipment is being investigated.
  • An issue where bulk open function is not available on Special Medal of Honor obtained from Twinkle's Diamond Box is being investigated.
  • An issue where a rope is placed at an abnormal location in Cache of Greed: Basement Level 3 - Area 3 is being investigated.
  • An issue where Red Stige's monster name contains text error is being investigated.
  • An issue where selecting Aquila in World Selection will always default to Channel 2 is being investigated.
  • An issue where Kanna's Ether Pulse's Ether Spot teleport cannot be used in Divine King Slime boss battle map is being investigated.
  • An issue when the character is being stunned in Lotus boss fight, excessive amount of text notice will appear if the character attempt to move is being investigated.
  • An issue where Seruf's Clam Bed appears abnormal is being investigated.

    • Happy Mapling!


    Dear Maplers,

    Please be informed that there will be a Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 30th October 2024, from 0900hrs to 1430hrs (GMT +8).
    Game services for all worlds will not be available during the stipulated time. Kindly log out before this period to avoid disruptions to your gameplay.

    Updates
  • Cash Shop Update details for 30th October 2024 can be found here.

    • Thank you.

    - MapleSEA Administrator

    Scheduled Maintenance - October 31, 2024


    We will be performing a scheduled maintenance Thursday, October 31, 2024 at 5:00 AM PDT (8:00 AM EDT / 1:00 PM CET / 11:00 PM AEDT). We anticipate the maintenance to last approximately 5 hours, concluding around 10:00 AM PDT (1:00 PM EDT / 6:00 PM CET / 4:00 AM AEDT November 1).

    Times:

    Thursday, October 31, 2024
    PDT (UTC -7): 5:00 AM - 10:00 AM
    EDT (UTC -4): 8:00 AM - 1:00 PM
    CET (UTC +1): 1:00 PM - 6:00 PMÂ 
    AEDT (UTC +10): 11:00 PM - 4:00 AM (November 1)

    • What will be unavailable:
      • All MapleStory game servers.
    • Changes and Updates (Additional Changes TBA):
      • Monthly Windows Update.
      • Resolved an issue so the Little Monster Block Show would not activate during Fireworks Festival. The players who used mesos before the fix but did not receive the buff will be compensated at a later date.
      • Resolved an issue that may cause Kanna players to disconnect when using Sol Janus: Dusk.
      • Resolved an issue when Cosmos was not activated properly, yet the cooldown being applied when Cosmic Burst was triggered while lagging.
      • Resolved an issue where the Dimensional Mirror in San Commerci was not teleporting players to the correct destination.
      • Resolved an issue where the chat window for 'Maple Fashion Week: Hallowkitty, Camila's Week' was showing incorrect text.

    In Interactive worlds, you can trade these style box items with other players through the Cash Item Trade window, if you haven't equipped them. Right-click on a character to see the menu and click on 'Trade Cash Item' button to trade unequipped PSSB items.

    You can also exchange them with Ari, located near the Free Market entrance, and receive a Style Box Stamp. You can receive one stamp per item. This stamp is permanent and untradeable. When you collect enough stamps, you can talk to Shiro, also located near the Free Market entrance, to exchange the stamps for a permanent equip item of your choice! PSSB items obtained in the Netherlands cannot be traded outside of the account, but can be traded within the account and be exchanged for Style Box Stamps.

    Open Wisp's Wondrous Wonderberry (available exclusively in Interactive worlds) to obtain one random 90-day pet or some pet-related consumables! Take home the Power XO Bun, Super XO Bun, and Magic XO Bun pets and summon them to obtain the XO Bun's Mysterious Power skill, which will increase your Weapon Attack and Magic Attack.

    Luna Crystal

    • PDT/PST (UTC -7/-8): Wednesday, October 9, 2024 (End of Maintenance) - Tuesday, November 5, 2024 11:59 PM PST
    • CEST/CET (UTC +2/+1): Wednesday, October 9, 2024 (End of Maintenance) - Wednesday, November 6, 2024 8:59 AM CET
    • AEDT (UTC +11): Wednesday, October 9, 2024 (End of Maintenance) - Wednesday, November 6, 2024 6:59 PM

    Available in Interactive worlds only:

    • Luna Crystal
      • Price (1): 3,900 NX
      • Duration: Permanent

    See all the rewards rates for this item here.

    Use the Luna Crystal (available exclusively in Interactive worlds) on a pair of Wonderberry pets to create a stronger buddy to help you out! By combining pets you get from Wisp's Wondrous Wonderberry or the Luna Crystal, you can get higher quality and more powerful 90-day pets!

    Use two Wonder Black pets, which can be obtained from Wisp's Wondrous Wonderberry, and receive either:

    • A Sweet Luna quality Power XO Bun, Super XO Bun, Magic XO Bun, Baby Hippo, Wolf Pup, Lion Cub, Dream Cloud, Dream Star, and Dream Moon 90-day pet.
    • A chance at a Petite Luna quality Florian, Florence, and Lil Flora 90-day pet.
    • Or the permanent Luna Crystal Key Pet Equipment, which can be used by any of the Petite Luna pets and give the appearance of their normal Pet Equipment!

    You can also combine a Wonder Black and Sweet Luna pet together and receive either:

    • A Dream Luna quality Power XO Bun, Super XO Bun, Magic XO Bun, Baby Hippo, Wolf Pup, Lion Cub, Dream Cloud, Dream Star, and Dream Moon 90-day pet.
    • Better chances at a Petite Luna quality Florian, Florence, and Lil Flora 90-day pet.
    • Or the permanent Luna Crystal Key Pet Equipment!

    Different quality pets grant different stat boosting skills when equipped as a set, instead of their normal pet set sklls:

    • Sweet Luna (Sweet Luna Skill): 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +6. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +14. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +24.
    • Dream Luna (Dream Luna Skill): 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +7. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +16. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +27.
    • Petite Luna (Butterfly Garden Skill): Comes with a Meso Magnet skill with a larger area of effect than normal. 1 pet grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +8. 2 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +18. 3 pets grants Weapon ATT/Magic ATT +30.

    In Interactive worlds, you can trade these style box items with other players through the Cash Item Trade window, if you haven't equipped them. Right-click on a character to see the menu and click on 'Trade Cash Item' button to trade unequipped PSSB items.

    You can also exchange them with Ari, located near the Free Market entrance, and receive a Style Box Stamp. You can receive one stamp per item. This stamp is permanent and untradeable. When you collect enough stamps, you can talk to Shiro, also located near the Free Market entrance, to exchange the stamps for a permanent equip item of your choice! Themed SSB items obtained in the Netherlands cannot be traded outside of the account, but can be traded within the account and be exchanged for Style Box stamps.
